        WHERE (([adoption].[AnimalId] = @__animalId_0) AND ([adoption].[AdopterId] = @__adopterId_1)) AND ([adoption].[AdoptionStatus] = @__adoptionStatus_2))
    THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
END
